 This statement of the Sangh chief meant that the way the party is campaigning for bjp's prime ministerial candidate Narendra Modi, individualism is dominating the party, and the RSS is not happy with it
 
 
 sangh pramukh kii baton se yah bhi laga ki vah bijepi main narendra modi ke badhate prabhaav se prasann nahin hai
 
 
 Having said this, Bhagwat has in a way favored those anti-modi leaders in the BJP, who are not happy with the growing influence of Narendra Modi in the party, and feel themselves slowly getting marginalized
 
 
 lekin, vaastaviktaa iske thik ulat he
 
 
 Mohan Bhagwat is known for giving lighthearted and quick reactions at times
 
 
 bhagwat ke is bayaan ke saath bhi aisa hi hua he, varanaa koi kaaran nahin ki jin bhagwat ke sangh pramukh rahete hue bijepi main peedi kaa badlaav hua, laalkrishna adwani jaise kaddavar netaa ke rahete hue narendra modi ko pradhanmantri pad kaa ummidavaar banaaya gaya, vah apni hi pasand ke khilaaf hazaar se zyaada prachaarkon ke saamne koi baat kahen
 
 
 It is not hidden that Narendra Modi has been made the choice of the prime ministerial candidate RSS
 
 
 modi ko yah jimmedaari dene se pehle mohan bhagwat ke kam se kam teen bade bayaan unke paksh main aae
 
 
 First, in Nashik, where after the interview of Bihar Chief Minister Nitish Kumar, he asked why there cannot be a Hindutva Prime Minister
 
 
 doosraa, meerut main, jahaan unhone kaha ki narendra modi ko pradhanmantri banane se koi nahin roak saktaa
 
 
 And Ti Sara, Allahabad Kumbh, where he publicly asked the BJP to pay attention to the sentiments of the country
 
 
 dilachasp baat yah he ki bengaluru main isi pratinidhi sabha kii baithak main teen din pehle sah-sarkarywah dattatreya hosbhole ne narendra modi kii ummidavaari kaa samarthan kiya tha
 
 
 He had said that Modi has been a volunteer of the Sangh and the Sangh is proud of him
 
 
 jabaki banaras or gandhinagar kii loksabhaa siton par hue vivaadon se murali manohar joshi or laalkrishna adwani kii naaraazgi par sangh ke sarkarywah bhaiyaji joshi ne ummid jataai thi ki bijepi ise hal kar legi
 
 
 BJP leaders say this is the first time since the elections held after the Emergency in 1977, when the Sangh became active to defeat the Congress
 
 
 kathith hindu aatankwaad ko lekar congress or sangh aamane-saamne hai
 
 
 Perhaps that is why Bhagwat also said that the question is not who should come at this time, rather the big question is who should not come
 
 
 aresas kaa maananaa he ki narendra modi ke naam par bijepi kaaryakartaon main josh aayaa he or bijepi modi ke netritv main congress ko haraa sakati he
 
 
 In the Lok Sabha elections 2014, the Sangh has also asked its workers to put in full force to ensure 100 percent voting
 
 
 varsh 2004 or 2009 ke loksabhaa chunaavon main bijepi kii shikaayat rahi thi ki sangh kaa cader gharon se baahar nahin niklaa, lekin is baar aisa hone kii sambhaavna kam he
 
 
 It is sure that the Sangh is against individualism, but its leaders believe that putting forward a face in electoral politics is part of a strategy
 
 
 khaastaur se tab, jab bijepi chunaav se pehle pradhanmantri pad kaa ummidavaar ghoshit kar inhen raashtrapati chunaav kii tarj par banane kii koshish karti rahi he
 
 
 Even before this, BJP had carried out a person-centric campaign while being the PM candidate of Atal Bihari Vajpayee and LK Advani
 
 
 so, ab modi ke naam ko ghar-ghar tak pahunchane ke liye bijepi ko 'namo-namo' karnaa pad rahaa he, lekin jahaan tak party main faisle lene kaa sawaal he, abhi tak aisa koi maamla nahin aayaa he, jab modi ne akele hi koi faisla kiya ho, balki narendra modi, rajnath singh, sushamaa swaraj, arun jetali, nitin gadakari, raamalaal jaise kai netaa milakar hi bade faisle kar rahe hai

 But whenever the police interacted with the woman, only one influential person who committed indecency with the woman was made an interpreter
 mahila ko har baar uske 'maalik' ko saunp diya jaataa or maalik ke parivaar ko badnaam karne ke liye use or adhik pratadit kiya jaataa, use dhamkee di jaati ki use peeche vaale bageeche main gaad diya jayega
 Three people were convicted on charges of torturing the woman for more than three years
 teenon vyaktiyon main se ek optician, ek kasaai or ek secretary he
 According to the newspaper report, the woman was exchanged between the three families and kept as a slave
 unhone mahila kaa passport jabt kar liya tha or ve mahila ko phooti kaudi bhi nahin dete the
 According to court documents, whenever the woman ran away and went to the police for help, her plea was ignored by the police
 aisa kam se kam 12 baar hua
 The woman's hellish life came to an end only after an organization working for migrant workers gave refuge to the woman and the human rights organization took up the issue of the woman
 abhiyojan paksh ke vakil carolin hophy ne cryden crown adaalat ke samaksh kaha, "anek sarkari sansthaaon ne uski sahaayta karne se inkaar kar diya, sahaayta ke liye mahila dwaara lagaai ja rahi baar-baar kii guhaar ko nazarandaaj kiya gaya, jaanch prakriya kaa paalan nahin kiya gaya or aisa kaha ja saktaa he ki sachai ko nazarandaaj kiya gaya
 " mahila apane jivan ko behatar banane tathaa bharat main apane parivaar ko kamakar rupee bhejne ke uddeshy se 2005 main bharat ke hyderabad se england pahunchi thi
 Whenever she tries to get someone's help, her 'boss' would harass her
 ek baar to ek peshewar dubhashie ne police ko bataaya ki mahila jhooth bol rahi he or uske desh main yah saamaanya baat he
 The woman was first taken to the hospital in 2006
 mahila kaa pair buree tarah jakhmi tha, kyonki uski 'malkin' shamina yusuf ne use cap se khinchakar maaraa tha
 The report said that no action was taken at that time, as the woman was threatened to tell someone about it
 mahila do varsh se bhi zyada samay ke baad bhaag gai, lekin apana passport lene ke liye vah us parivaar ke duusare rishtedaaron ke paas waapas laut gai
 The woman's lawyer told the court that the woman lived in a one-room house in St
 John's Wood and was raped by the butcher, Ankarta Balapovi, several times
 mahila kisi tarah bhaag gai or uskaa maamla england kii scotland yard police kii taskari ikai ko saunp diya gaya
 The comments optician balram oberoi or secretary yusuf ko mahila ke saath marpet ke liye doshi qaraar diya gaya
 Oberoi was also found guilty of threatening to kill him
 vahiin kasaai, balapovi ko dushkarm kaa doshi paaya gaya
 He will be sentenced next month
 do anya prativaadiyon ko chhod diya gaya
 The victim is so injured due to the assault that she has to resort to wheelchair

 adalati dastavej ke anusaar mahila jab bhi bhagkar police ke paas sahaayta ke liye gai, uski yachana ko police ne nazarandaaj kar diya
 This happened at least 12 times
 pravasi kamgaaron ke liye kaam karne vaali ek sanstha dwaara mahila ko sharan die jane or maanavadhikaar sanghathan dwaara mahila kaa mudda apane haath main liye jane ke baad hi mahila ke naarkeey jivan kaa ant ho sakaa
 Prosecuting lawyer Carolyn Hoffie said before Croydon Crown Court, "many governmental entities refuse to assist her, repeated pleas by woman for help, ignored, not followed by investigative process It was done and it can be said that the truth was ignored
 " The woman arrived in England from Hyderabad, India in 2005 with the aim of improving her life and sending money to her family in India
 vah jab bhi kisi kii sahaayta praapt karne kii koshish karti, uske 'maalik' use pratadit karte

 mahila ko pehali baar 2006 main aspataal le jaaya gaya

 rapat main kaha gaya he ki haalanki us samay koi karrwai nahi kii gai, kyonki mahila ko iske bare main kisi ko bataane ke liye dhamkaaya gaya tha
 The woman escaped after more than two years, but returned to other relatives of the family to get her passport
 mahila ke vakil ne adaalat ko bataaya ki mahila saint johns wood main ek kamare vaale makaan main rahati thi or kasaai, ankarta balapovi ne uske saath kai baar dushkarm kiya
 The woman somehow escaped and her case was handed over to the trafficking unit of Scotland Yard Police in England

 pehle sarkaar ne kaha ki rashtriya suraksha ko dekhte hue saude kaa detail nahin diya ja saktaa he, lekin baad main yaad dilaayaa gaya ki raksha rajya mantri to november 2016 main hi sansad main rafaal vimaan kaa daam bataa chuke the
 Recently, Arun Jaitley has surrounded the Congress by writing a blog
 uske baad videsh rajya mantri emje akbar ne bhi lekh likhaa he
 We will talk briefly about the questions and claims raised in those articles, but first lets hear why Prashant Bhushan held a press conference today
 arun shouri, yashavanth sinha or prashanth bhushan ke sawaal par sarkaar se kisi ne bhi blog nahin likhaa he
 In his blog, Arun Jaitley has only asked the Congress that the process goes on for 10 years on the Rafale deal
 kya isse rashtriya suraksha se samjhauta nahin hua
 Was the delay caused by Bofors looking for a transaction opportunity? jaahir he jetali is deree ko rashtriya suraksha se hue samjhaute se jodate hai to jetali ko yah bhi bataanaa chahie ki jis vayusena ko rashtriya suraksha ke liye 126 rafaal chahie the, use ab 36 kyon chahie
 The question which Prashant Bhushan is raising
 sarkaar kii taraf se bhi jo daam bataae gaye hai usamen samay samay par antar dekha gaya he
 But Arun Jaitley has raised the issue of different prices in Rahul Gandhi's statements, except for these differences
 doordarshan ko die intervyuu main deal sin hone ke teen din baad tab ke raksha mantri kehete hai ki unhen jaankaree nahin he
 On 10 April 2015, two days before the deal was signed, the then foreign secretary says that Hindustan Aeronautics Limited was involved in the deal
 dasso company ke si i o kaa bhi bayaan chhapata he ki ech e el prakriya main shaamil he
 But when the deal is signed the whole process changes
 yah sab prashanth bhushan ne pehle ke press conference main bataaya tha
 Now the Defense Minister himself never responded to this
 unki jagah vitt mantri ne blog likhaa
 Asked 15 questions to Congress
 blog main jetali bataa rahe hai ki upie ke samay 126 aircraft kharidne kii prakriya ek dashak tak chali
 Then he does not tell in this blog how the issue has come down from 126 to 36, which is being asked by Prashant Bhushan
 jetali apane blog main likhte hai ki 10 april 2015 ko bharat or france kii sarkaar ne saajha bayaan jari kiya tha or bharat ne tay kiya ki pehle se behatar sharton par 36 rafaal kharide jaaenge
 On 13 May 2015, the Defense Acquisition Council approved and after going through the extensive process, the deal is signed on 23 September 2016
 prashanth bhushan to yahi puch rahe hai ki kya airforce ne likhakar diya ki 126 kii jagah hamen 36 chahie
 Was there a rethink in the committees made for this? jetali ke blog se zaahir hota he ki saajha ghoshnaa patr ke elaan ke baad ek maheene baad dephence equisshan council manzuri detii he
 So, is Prashant Bhushan saying that keeping everyone in the dark was announced in the Common Manifesto
 29 agast ke hi blog main jetali likhte hai ki kya rahul gandhi ko pataa tha ki 2007 main kitna daam tha
 Did he know that its terms included price increases
 jiske anusaar 2015 main jab deal sin kiya to prati jahaaz daam bad jate
 NDA has done the deal at 9% lower price
 aap dekhenge ki jetali bhi apane blog main nahin bataate ki hai ki ek jahaaz kii kya keemat he
 If the price of the ship is being asked, Jaitley says that Rafal was purchased at 9 percent less price during the time of NDA
 kya unhen maaloom tha ki 2007 kaa daam kya he, agar maaloom he to blog main kyon nahin likhaa
 Whereas he asks Rahul Gandhi in the blog whether he knows the price fixed in 2007
 jetali iskaa jawaab dete hai ki deal main koi privet company kaise aa gai
 It is said that the condition was made at the time of UPA that the original manufacturer company can partner itself with the Indian company to supply or maintain the components in India
 iskaa sarkaar se koi lenaa dena nahin he
 But the answer could not be found as to why the Dasso aviation company, which makes Rafale, would partner a company whose experience in this field is quite new and it is alleged that the company came into existence only a few months ago
 jetali is pahalu ko nahin choote hai
 Jaitley has responded in his blog that it has been discussed by the Price Negotiation Committee and Contract Negotiation Committee for 14 months before the deal sign
 cabinet kamity on security kii manjuuri lee gai
 Now come to the point of election of offset companies
 reliance ne apana jo jawaab media ko bheja tha, usamen likhaa tha ki dasso aviation use akele 30,000 karod kaa theka nahin diya he
 How much work will be received has not been decided yet
 dasso aviation ne 100 se adhik companiyon ko kaam dene ke liye ishaara kiya he
 It has both HAL and Bharat Electronics Limited
 tippaniyan Jaitley's blog on which MJ Akbar has written in the Times of India does not name Hindustan Aeronautics Limited
 akbar likhte hai ki tathy yah he ki 72 aisi companiyaan hai jinamein bharat electronics or diardio bhi he or privet company tata bhi he
 30,000 crore orders will be distributed among these 72 companies
 kya rahul gandhi yah samajhate hai ki 72 companiyon ko milane vaale 30,000 karod ke kaam se koi company 45000 karod kaa munafa kaise kama sakati he
 HAL is named in response to Reliance
 emje akbar ke lekh main echeel kaa naam nahin he
 Then the number of companies in response to Reliance is 100 and in response to the government the number of companies is 72
 kisko sahi maaloom he yah is baat par nirbhar karata he ki sawaal poochne par sabase pehle manahani kaa daawa koun karata he
 We have Yashwant Sinha with whom we will talk
 arun shouri, yashavanth sinha or prashanth bhushan ke sawaal par sarkaar se kisi ne bhi blog nahin likhaa he
